"role": "user", "name": "Reasoning"}, {"content": "{\"message\":\"The code snippet solves the given initial value problem for the second-order linear ODE with constant coefficients. It computes the solution u(t) using the characteristic roots, applies the initial conditions to find constants, and then finds the smallest time T such that |u(t)| \u2264 0.1 for all t > T.
